    async def test_multi_service_cascading_health_check(self):
        """娴嬭瘯澶氭湇鍔＄骇鑱斿仴搴锋鏌ュ満鏅?""
        # 瀵煎叆骞跺垱寤烘鏌ュ櫒
        try:
            from src.infrastructure.health.components.enhanced_health_checker import EnhancedHealthChecker
    
            class TestChecker(EnhancedHealthChecker):
                def check_service(self, name):
                    return {"service": name, "status": "healthy"}
    
                async def check_service_async(self, name):
                    await asyncio.sleep(0.001)
                    return self.check_service(name)
    
            checker = TestChecker()
        except Exception:
            pass  # Skip condition handled by mock/import fallback
            return
    
        # 1. 妯℃嫙鏈嶅姟渚濊禆閾撅細database -> cache -> api -> web
        services = ["database", "cache", "api", "web"]
    
        # 2. 鎵ц绾ц仈妫€鏌?
        results = []
        for service in services:
            result = await checker.check_service_async(service)
            results.append(result)
            # 楠岃瘉姣忎竴姝ラ兘鎴愬姛
            assert result["status"] == "healthy"
    
        # 3. 楠岃瘉瀹屾暣閾捐矾
        assert len(results) == len(services)
    
        # 4. 妫€鏌ユ暣浣撳仴搴风姸鎬?

    def test_cpu_usage_threshold_check(self):

            CPU_USAGE_WARNING_THRESHOLD,

        )
    
        test_cases = [
            (45.0, HEALTH_STATUS_HEALTHY),
            (85.0, HEALTH_STATUS_WARNING),

    def check_service(self, name: str, timeout: float = 5.0) -> HealthCheckResult:
        """妫€鏌ュ崟涓湇鍔?""
        start_time = time.time()

            if name not in self._health_checks:
                return HealthCheckResult(
                    service_name=name,
                    status="error",
                    timestamp=datetime.now(),
                    response_time=time.time() - start_time,
                    details={"error": f"鏈嶅姟 {name} 鏈敞鍐?},
                    recommendations=["鍏堟敞鍐岃鏈嶅姟"]
                )

                service_name=name,

                details=result,
                recommendations=self._generate_recommendations(result)
            )

            return health_result

            def db_check():

                    CheckType.CONNECTIVITY,
                    details={"db_status": "connected"}
                )
            return db_check

                )
            return cache_check

    def test_performance_under_concurrent_load(self, checker):
        """娴嬭瘯骞跺彂璐熻浇涓嬬殑鎬ц兘"""
        import threading
        import time
    
        # 娉ㄥ唽澶氫釜鏈嶅姟
        for i in range(10):
            service_name = f"perf_service_{i}"
            def create_check(service_id=i):
                def check():
                    time.sleep(0.01)  # 妯℃嫙妫€鏌ユ椂闂?
                    return {"status": "healthy", "message": f"Service {service_id} OK"}
                return check
    
            checker.register_service(service_name, create_check())
    
        # 骞跺彂妫€鏌ユ墍鏈夋湇鍔?
        results = {}
        exceptions = []
    
        def check_worker(service_name: str):
            try:
                start_time = time.time()
                result = checker.check_service(service_name)
                end_time = time.time()
                results[service_name] = (result, end_time - start_time)
            except Exception as e:
                exceptions.append(f"{service_name}: {e}")
    
        threads = []
        for i in range(10):
            service_name = f"perf_service_{i}"
            t = threading.Thread(target=check_worker, args=(service_name,))
            threads.append(t)
            t.start()
    
        # 绛夊緟鎵€鏈夌嚎绋嬪畬鎴?
        for t in threads:
            t.join(timeout=5.0)
    
        # 涓嶅簲璇ユ湁寮傚父

    def test_performance_under_load(self, checker):
        """娴嬭瘯璐熻浇涓嬬殑鎬ц兘琛ㄧ幇"""
        import threading
    
        results = []
        errors = []
    
        def worker():
            try:
                # 鎵ц鍋ュ悍妫€鏌?
                result = asyncio.run(checker._check_performance_metrics_async("test_service"))
                results.append(result)
            except Exception as e:
                errors.append(e)
    
        # 鍚姩澶氫釜绾跨▼妯℃嫙骞跺彂璐熻浇
        threads = []
        for i in range(5):
            t = threading.Thread(target=worker)
            threads.append(t)
            t.start()
    
        # 绛夊緟鎵€鏈夌嚎绋嬪畬鎴?
        for t in threads:
            t.join()
    
        # 楠岃瘉缁撴灉
>       assert len(results) == 5, f"Expected 5 results, got {len(results)}"
E       AssertionError: Expected 5 results, got 0

    @classmethod
    def create_health_checker(cls,
                              checker_type: str = 'basic',
                              config: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None):
        """
        鍒涘缓鍋ュ悍妫€鏌ュ櫒瀹炰緥
    
        Args:
            checker_type: 妫€鏌ュ櫒绫诲瀷 ('basic', 'enhanced', 'fastapi')
            config: 閰嶇疆瀛楀吀
    
        Returns:
            鍋ュ悍妫€鏌ュ櫒瀹炰緥
    
        Raises:
            ValueError: 涓嶆敮鎸佺殑妫€鏌ュ櫒绫诲瀷
        """
        if checker_type not in cls.SUPPORTED_TYPES:
            supported_types = ', '.join(cls.SUPPORTED_TYPES.keys())
            raise ValueError(f"涓嶆敮鎸佺殑妫€鏌ュ櫒绫诲瀷: {checker_type}. 鏀寔鐨勭被鍨? {supported_types}")
    
        checker_class = cls.SUPPORTED_TYPES[checker_type]
    
        try:
            if checker_type == 'fastapi':
                # FastAPI妫€鏌ュ櫒闇€瑕佸厛鍒涘缓鍩虹妫€鏌ュ櫒
                base_checker = cls.create_health_checker('enhanced', config)
                checker = checker_class(base_checker, config)
